Special Article

Abstract Translation of the Sixth Compilation of the Feetham Report

(4)

An excerpt from Sun Chuanfang's speech in Shanghai on May 5, 1926, is cited to indicate the opposition of Chinese officials at the time to the expansion of the Public Concession or the construction of roads beyond the concession. The establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government in July 1927 is also mentioned in the report. The establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Government was the only Chinese municipal organ in Shanghai. The municipal government requested that the land of the roads beyond the concession and its adjacent areas be placed under its jurisdiction as part of the municipal government's area. The existence of the Public Concession's roads beyond the concession and the administrative measures taken by the bureau within the roads beyond the concession and its adjacent areas are an obstacle to the newly established Chinese municipal government's exercise of its functions in these areas and seem to be considered a permanent enemy of its functions. The desire of the Chinese municipal government to expand its scope of activities has led to the simultaneous exercise of functions by two organs in the same area, and various difficult problems have arisen as a result. I firmly believe that one thing must be admitted, that is, as far as the Public Concession itself is concerned, if the powers granted to the bureau by the Land Regulations are frankly acknowledged, the conflict between the two organs can obviously be avoided. However, considering the situation of the officials of the newly established Chinese municipal government, this kind of conflict is indeed practically unavoidable. The influence of politics and the party department has aggravated the difficulties inherent in the situation at the time and made the work of the representatives of both authorities, who all believed it was appropriate to negotiate a kind of temporary solution, even more complicated. The Public Security Bureau of the Shanghai Municipal Government, in order to effectively exercise its functions on a certain road beyond the concession, established police stations at locations adjacent to each road and sent armed police officers to patrol each road. One of their duties to be carried out at any time was to stop the work being carried out by the Public Concession's Public Works Department on each road. The Public Concession Bureau, in order to avoid any dangerous conflict between the two police organs, has since then no longer insisted on its claims to the roads that clearly belonged to the bureau, and the repair work needed for each road that had been stopped has also been put on hold. Before this work was recently established through friendly measures by both sides, the maintenance of most roads beyond the concession had been temporarily suspended, and some roads had even become almost impassable. The exercise of the rights granted to the public utility companies of the Public Concession within the area of the roads beyond the concession by the special franchise contracts signed between the companies and the bureau, was a problem that arose between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the companies. The current situation of the police on the roads beyond the concession is discussed in the report as follows: The municipal government police on duty on the roads beyond the concession are a group of trained people, and the Public Concession police officers who are often in contact within each area usually get along well with each other. However, the fact that two groups of armed officers are separately under the command of two authorities competing for jurisdiction and want to exercise police power and patrol the same road in the same area is inherently dangerous and easily seen. The municipal government police officers, in cases involving foreigners, mostly use intimidation tactics when trying to exercise their functions, partly due to a lack of experience and unfamiliarity with foreign languages, which has led to various difficulties. In addition to this kind of danger and difficulty, the necessary work to maintain each road and the business of each public utility company are hindered. From the point of view of the general public's interests, the current situation is extremely inconvenient and cannot be considered satisfactory by the authorities concerned.

Chapter 3

A special discussion of "The Current Situation and the Interests Involved" includes various statistical tables relating to all points related to the land of the roads beyond the concession. The nature of the residents of the land of the roads beyond the concession and the extent to which the residents of the Public Concession often travel to this land are discussed as follows: The Chinese and foreign residents living on the roads beyond the concession and its adjacent areas are actually an integral part of the residents of the Public Concession from both a social and economic point of view. Most of the foreign households and most of the Chinese households in the area of the roads beyond the concession are employed in the Public Concession during the day. The Chinese and foreign residents in the Public Concession are heavily dependent on the land of the roads beyond the concession as a place for recreation. In addition to Zhaofeng Park in the Western District and Hongkou Park and the playground in the Northern District, which were all established by the bureau, there is also a swimming pool established by the bureau in the Northern District, and private sports clubs in the Western District. The roads beyond the concession in the Western District are still mostly built with soil, probably for the purpose of racing. Therefore, in addition to the residents who actually live on the land of the roads beyond the concession, the Chinese and foreign residents in the Public Concession who often go to the land of the roads beyond the concession for entertainment and recreation are very numerous. And many, probably go every day. The administrative facilities of the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Public Concession Bureau on the land of the roads beyond the concession are all described. The construction of Zhongshan Road by the Shanghai Municipal Government in the Western District and the administrative measures in the Northwest and Northern Districts are also mentioned. Then another statistical table is mentioned, which is a list of the basic amount of money actually invested by the Public Concession Bureau in real estate projects and buildings on the land of the roads beyond the concession. And citing the numbers opened in the table, it shows that the basic investment of the bureau in these two areas is a total of Taels 10,039,110. Among them, Taels 2,894,660 were used for the price of the land used for road construction and the basic cost of building roads and their auxiliary projects. Another thing to be noted is that the numbers listed in the table are all based on the price of the land at the time of requisition and the cost of construction at the time of construction. The initial or main purpose of the projects undertaken by the Public Concession Bureau on the land of the roads beyond the concession was to seek benefits for the landlords and residents of each area. The nature and cost of this project are described in detail. And it is stated that the special donations collected by the bureau from the residents of the land of the roads beyond the concession are only slightly more than half of the estimated cost of the projects undertaken. But it is pointed out that when preparing the budget for each area, the part of the franchise fee paid by the bureau and each public utility company from the operating income in each area should be regarded as the local income of each area, which is fair. The amount of money that should be regarded as the local income of each area is estimated to be about Taels 175,000 per year. The report then points out that the projects undertaken by the Public Concession Bureau on the land of the roads beyond the concession, the projects built, and the cost of each project are listed in detail in the statistical table, which does not represent all of the administrative benefits of the Public Concession obtained by the residents of the roads beyond the concession. The residents of the land of the roads beyond the concession who pay municipal taxes to the bureau, in addition to the special benefits of the projects directly undertaken by the bureau in each area, also obtain various benefits. These residents can go to the bureau's hospitals for medical treatment, visit the bureau's parks, and send their children to the bureau's schools. The Public Concession's control of food through public health methods, as well as the services of various public utility companies under the supervision of the Public Concession authorities to a certain extent, are all beneficial to these residents. The taxes paid by these residents to pay for the various municipal administration is much smaller than what must be paid by those living within the Public Concession. The houses they live in are exempt from land tax, and the house tax they pay is also 2% lower than what is levied in the Public Concession. In terms of the amount of tax that must be borne, I believe that the residents and property owners of the land of the roads beyond the concession have been in a position that is too favorable to this day. The residents and property owners of the land of the roads beyond the concession enjoy various less obvious benefits because each area is adjacent to the Public Concession. The safety of the Public Concession enjoyed by these people is not insignificant. They also directly or indirectly benefit from the rule of law and the two principles of autonomy adopted by the Public Concession. As far as the relationship between these people and the bureau is concerned, the respect for their personal and property rights, the taxes they pay should be established according to a uniform and definite standard based on resolutions discussed and approved by the public, and the use and reimbursement of the taxes collected should be handled in the same way as those paid by the residents and property owners in the Public Concession, all of which have been guaranteed by the bureau. The residents and property owners of the land of the roads beyond the concession directly or indirectly enjoy various benefits due to the existence and activities of the Public Concession administration. The industrial value of each area has naturally also increased. However, although this benefit is great, in terms of the land price that has already been mentioned, there is a very real distinction between the industry within the Public Concession and the industry on the land of the roads beyond the concession. Once you cross the boundary line of the concession, the industrial value is reduced by 20%. This is due to the difference in safety between the Public Concession and the area beyond the concession. Regarding the general situation of all the existing and future interests of the bureau on the land of the roads beyond the concession, it is stated as follows: The existing interests of the bureau and the Public Concession society on the land of the roads beyond the concession, the amount of which is huge, and the variety of which is numerous, have already been described in detail. I believe that if the Public Concession still maintains its importance as a commercial and industrial center, and its population continues to increase, then the importance of each area to the Public Concession in the future will be much greater than it is now. The Public Concession society must obtain a kind of land in the adjacent places that can be reached by the Kangzhuang Avenue to be used for development. This kind of land must have both residential and business places, and the administrative situation of the land can attract residents and encourage the development of commerce. The tendency of the Public Concession headquarters to be too crowded is increasing with each year. It is still possible to create a residential area in the areas beyond the concession that can attract residents. There is a hope that a large-scale garden-style suburb can be developed to make the facilities for a happy life better than those in the crowded and unbearable Public Concession. The high land prices in the Public Concession have made houses expensive and the business burden has also been increased somewhat. However, the extent to which the landlords in the Public Concession enjoy the monopoly land price depends largely on the situation outside the concession. If the safety of each area adjacent to the concession is reduced or the administration is corrupt, it will make the land price in the Public Concession even higher. On the contrary, if the situation in the adjacent areas is improved, at least part of the monopoly value of the real estate in the Public Concession will be stripped away, and its land price will fall. There is also a problem, which is that for the benefit of the residents of the Public Concession, it is necessary to obtain bases to be used as various public places, such as schools, hospitals, and the most important sports fields. The Chinese society is becoming increasingly popular with various games and sports. If it is not in a large area near the Public Concession that can be reached by the avenue, the difficulty of expanding the convenience of sports will increase with each day. Under the existing situation, there is a great danger that the opportunity for future development will be lost due to the lack of sufficiently effective administration in the area of the roads beyond the concession. Therefore, a plan for constructing the city must be planned to ensure that the existing development of the land of the roads beyond the concession can proceed along a satisfactory path. The report then mentions that the benefits of the Shanghai Municipal Government on the land of the roads beyond the concession "belong to potential storage and there is no actual." And mentions the benefits of various public utility companies. The various interests that must be considered are outlined as follows: Any future administrative plan for the roads beyond the concession will affect public and private interests. This interest can be broadly divided into the following categories: (1) The interests of Chinese and foreign private households and property owners on the roads beyond the concession or in its adjacent areas, including the interests of factory owners. (2) The interests of the villagers living in the areas surrounded by the roads beyond the concession or served by the roads beyond the concession. (3) The interests of various public utility companies. (4) The interests of the bureau and the residents of the Public Concession. (5) The interests of the Shanghai Municipal Government. I believe that one thing must be admitted, that is, the benefits obtained by all the residents, individual property owners, and all the residents of the Public Concession in each area within the land of the roads beyond the concession have grown up under a kind of governance. No matter whether the legal basis of this kind of governance is sufficient or not, there may be any questions. The development that has gone through many years is mostly purely out of the pressure of needs. And not only has given great benefits to the Public Concession and its residents, but also to the land directly related to it and the villagers in the areas adjacent to it.

Chapter 4

Discussing suggestions for the future. The requirements for any plan to be adopted for the future administration of the roads beyond the concession are stated as follows: I believe that the main purpose of this plan should be stated as follows: that is, the conflict that has arisen due to the mutual contention between the two sides for the administrative power of the roads beyond the concession should be eliminated, and sufficient regulations should be established to ensure that each area has effective administration and development in the future. In order to achieve this purpose and plan the plan to be adopted, considerable attention must be paid to political considerations. But I believe that there is also an important relationship that must be admitted, that is, no matter what this plan is, the legal claims and interests created by past history and the current situation for all the authorities, public utility companies, and all the residents and property owners, as well as the interests of the Public Concession society and the residents of its adjacent areas, should be fairly recognized as the basis of this plan to the extent that the land of the roads beyond the concession is mutually related. Five alternative methods for dealing with the future of the land of the roads beyond the concession, which have been proposed or considered at various times, are summarized. The first two methods are as follows: (1) Expand the Public Concession to include the land of the roads beyond the concession. (2) The Public Concession abandons any claim to participate in the administration of each area, abolishes the concession police officers in each area, and stops the concession administration in each area. The above two methods, because they cede the legal claims and interests of party A to party B, have both been discarded. The third alternative method is to divide the land of the roads beyond the concession between the Shanghai Municipal Government and the Public Concession Bureau for management, that is, part is merged into the Public Concession, and the remaining part is completely governed by the Shanghai Municipal Government. This method has also been rejected. Because the general Chinese opinion does not agree with any expansion of the Public Concession. And from the Public Concession's point of view, any plan that would allow the Public Concession to completely cede all interests outside the railway tracks (i.e., the proposed boundary line) in the Western District cannot be considered satisfactory due to the nature of the existing interests of the Public Concession in this part of the Western District and the extent to which the future development of the concession must be affected. The remaining two methods are discussed as follows: In addition, there are two other alternative methods, that is, adopting some form of joint administration and creating a new organ. I believe that the most promising way to solve the administrative problem of the land of the roads beyond the concession is to adopt some form of joint administration first, and hope that a more comprehensive plan can be adopted later to establish a new organ for the administration of the land of the roads beyond the concession. Therefore, I suggest that one thing must be admitted, that is, the various problems involved must be dealt with in two phases. In the first phase, there cannot be a complete and final solution. Only the plan adopted in the first phase that is helpful for the time being should be planned so that it can guide the second phase to adopt a more comprehensive and more permanent plan. (End)

Important News

Jiaohe Ninth Normal School Teachers and Students Go on Hunger Strike to Petition

Tianjin, 12th telegram: The students of Jiaohe Ninth Normal School previously elected representatives last month to come to Tianjin to request the removal of Principal Sang Danfeng. Zhang Jian'an, the director of the Education Department, detained the petitioning representatives and has not released them yet. The students were greatly angered and elected 40 more representatives to walk north to Tianjin on the 12th. They immediately went to the Provincial Government to petition for the release of the students and the removal of the principal, but they were unsuccessful. As a result, the students became even more angry and have decided to go on a complete hunger strike from today onwards. If they do not achieve victory, they vow to fight to the death. According to the representatives, their school was forced to leave the school on the 9th by Li Fuhe of the Fifth Brigade, together with County Magistrate Liu Yangyan, leading an armed platoon. Otherwise, they would all be shot. More than 300 students could only cry and leave the school, lodging in broken temples, without money to return home. Today, they met Director Zhang to request the restoration of the school, or to issue travel expenses so that the students can return home, but they were rejected. The colleagues appealed with a hunger strike, hoping to move the director to pity. If there is no solution tomorrow, they will send a letter inviting all the students to come to Tianjin and starve to death at the Education Department.

Tsinghua Announces Presidents of Three Colleges

Beiping, 11th telegram: Weng Wenhao, the acting president of Tsinghua, today announced the presidents of the three colleges: 1. College of Liberal Arts, Feng Youlan; 2. College of Law, Chen Zong; 3. College of Science, Ye Qisun. Ye is currently abroad and is temporarily represented by Wu Zhengzhi.

Preparatory Committee for the National Vocational Education Conference

The preparatory meeting for the National Vocational Education Conference, convened by the China Vocational Education Society, was held at the Zhenjiang Women's Vocational School at 3 PM on the 11th. Attendees included Leng Yuqiu, Qi Yisan, Feng Maiying, Yang Weiyu, Lu Yuqing, Ren Zhongmin, Jin Shubai, Fa Shenzhong, Zhou Kaisen, Qin Fengxiang, Zhang Yiyun, Wu Cuilun, Liu Jianxing, and Xu Yian. Leng Yuqiu chaired the meeting, with Wu Cuilun as the recorder. After formal greetings, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting. Yang Weiyu and Wu Cuilun reported on the preparations, including (1) the reasons for changing the venue of this conference, (2) the filing with the Jiangsu Provincial Government, (3) the approval of reduced train and boat fares by the Ministry of Railways and Communications, and (4) the registration of approximately 150 representatives and members. Matters for discussion included one item: the organizational plan for this preparatory committee. It was resolved that the organization would be as follows: General Affairs Section, divided into Documentation, Accounting, and General Services groups; Conference Section, divided into Recording, Printing, and Organizing groups; Public Relations Section, divided into Reception, Accommodation, and Excursion groups. It was also resolved regarding the allocation of duties that Zhang Yiyun and Fa Shenzhong would be the chief officers of the General Affairs Section, Jin Shubai and Feng Maiying would be the chief officers of the Conference Section, and Qi Yisan and Liu Jianxing would be the chief officers of the Public Relations Section. The assistant staff for each section were as follows: Documentation: Wu Cuilun; Accounting: Yang Fengshu; General Services: Xu Yian, Cai Yanru, Zhou Kaisen; Recording: Pan Yangyao, Yao Huiquan, Jiang Zhuoqun; Printing: Jin Wen'ao, Feng Maiying; Organizing: Jin Shubai, Wu Cuilun, Lu Yuqing; Public Relations: Temporarily not divided into groups, Qin Fengxiang, Ren Zhongmin, Zhang Xiuhe, Huang Bingpei, Zhou Kaisen, Bao Mingshu, Yi Jianlou. Another item was the location of the office. It was resolved that it would be at the Women's Vocational School before the 29th and move to Boxian Park from the 29th. Another item was the conference schedule. It was resolved that it would be drafted by the society's office. Another item was the public recommendation of the conference presidium. It was resolved to recommend the following: Cai Jiemin, Chen Bulei, Ye Chucang, Leng Yuqiu, Hu Shuhua. If Mr. Hu is unavailable, Jiang Wenyu will act as his proxy. Another item was the budget for the conference. It was resolved to ask Yang Weiyu to prepare a total budget of 1200 to 1500 yuan.

Record of the International Agricultural Conference (2)

(Sent by Mr. Tang Huisun, Chinese Representative, from Prague)

Resolutions

The conference proposals were the sole task of this session. The proposals were proposed by various members last year and decided by the International Agricultural Commission at a meeting in Brussels, Belgium in August last year. The proposals for this conference are divided into seven groups: (1) Agricultural Policy and Agricultural Economics, (2) Agricultural Education and Publicity, (3) Agricultural Cooperation, (4) Plant Production, (5) Animal Production, (6) Agricultural Technology, (7) Rural Women. The important proposals are as follows: 1. How to balance the supply and demand of agricultural products in various countries. 2. The dissemination of various modern wireless telephones, movies, agricultural exhibitions, etc. to rural areas. 3. Agricultural cooperation training should focus on practical application and excellent results. 4. Investigate the current situation and progress of agricultural cooperation in the world. 5. New varieties obtained through selection breeding must be legally protected from a national and international standpoint. 6. How to apply genetic theory to improve the economic production of livestock. 7. Management and production of fish ponds. 8. How to balance the market supply and demand of potato processing and preservation. 9. The role of women in rural prosperity. 10. Rationalization of farm household management (home economics). A total of seventeen proposals were discussed in group meetings over several days, resulting in appropriate solutions to solve various important international agricultural problems in modern times.

Travel and Sightseeing

The conference organizing committee has a travel and sightseeing group dedicated to handling the travel and sightseeing of members and representatives. During the conference, groups are divided to visit sites outside of meeting hours. Guides who can speak German, French, and Czech explain separately. For several days, they visited famous sites in Prague and agricultural vocational schools, cooperative unions, the Czech agricultural exhibition, and rural areas near Prague. In addition, after the conference, they divided into six groups to investigate agriculture in various parts of the Czech Republic. I also joined the visit for six days to observe the overview of cooperative areas in Czech rural areas.

Czech Hospitality

Czech President Masaryk is a scholar with prominent political achievements, praised by the world. The Czech people love and respect him very much. Statues of the President are built everywhere in Prague, and portraits of the President are hung everywhere. The depth of their respect can be seen. This International Agricultural Conference was held in the Czech Republic, and President Masaryk gave it great consideration. Representatives of various governments were received by Czech government officials. The President also held regular receptions and banquets for the Minister of Foreign Affairs and the Minister of Agriculture.

The conference was held in Prague for four days, and the closing ceremony was held on the afternoon of June 8. The proposals of each group were read out one by one and unanimously approved by the audience. The conference has resolved that the 16th International Agricultural Conference will be held in Budapest, the capital of Hungary, in 1933. I will report on the conference proposals separately in the future, as these resolutions are quite important and worthy of our country's participation. I sincerely hope that our country's authorities will pay special attention to this type of international conference. The representatives attending each conference should be designated as soon as possible, so that they can prepare early and make suggestions at the conference, or receive information on the improvement of agriculture in our country and introduce it to the conference to enhance the international agricultural status. (End)

School News Digest

Junyi Middle School This Junyi Middle School was founded in July 1928. The city's Education Bureau approved its establishment in October 1929. It was originally established to commemorate martyr Zhang Junyi. Its founders are all members of this Party Department, such as Wu Kaixian and Chen Xihhao. Most of the school board members are famous figures in Shanghai's business community, such as Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, and Xu Jilun. It has been established for three years now. Most of the students who have graduated from the school have served in Party departments at all levels and various mass organizations, which is quite commendable. This year, the Ministry of Education has granted its approval for filing due to the school's outstanding performance.

Chinese Vocational Education Society Japanese Language Association The modern Japanese language summer intensive course attached to the Chinese Vocational Education Society has already started. The teaching method is novel and the course lasts for seven weeks.

Huhai Elementary School Huhai Elementary School on North Xizang Road has been expanding since last year and has hired Mr. Xu Huimin as the Director of Student Affairs. The management is strict. The sixth graduating class of the school held its graduation ceremony yesterday afternoon at 3 PM. About 600 people, including school board member Shen Lianfang and students' families, attended. World Tennis Queen Madam Matty Plans to Tour the East for Performances

Approximately After the US National Tennis Championships

San Francisco, 10th - Madam Matty Weills stated that she is considering a tour of the East. The Japan Lawn Tennis Association has invited her to perform in Japan, and she feels that the time is ripe. Madam Matty hopes to give several performances in China, Japan, and the Philippines, approximately after participating in the Anglo-American Women's Wightman Cup tennis competition and the US National Tennis Championships. Madam Matty is a Californian who has held the World Women's Tennis Championship for many years. Important world women's championships such as the French Tennis Championships and the Wimbledon Tennis Championships have all been won by her. Since her marriage last year, she has not been able to go to England due to family affairs, resulting in the Wimbledon women's singles championship, which she had held for four years, being won by German Miss Olsen. This year, she is preparing to win back the Wightman Cup and the American women's singles championship from the English women.

Record of the Jiangnan Track and Field Team's Northern Expedition (2)

| From Nanjing to Tianjin |

The Jiangnan Northern Expedition Track and Field Team arrived safely in Tianjin on the evening of the 30th and stayed at Nankai Middle School. The situation along the way is described as follows:

Athletes Cross the Yangtze River and Show Their True Colors

On the evening of the 28th, for the convenience of crossing the Yangtze River the next day, the entire team moved to the Dazhi Building Hotel by the river and rested. On the morning of the 29th, they got up at 5:30 AM and finished breakfast. Then, they crossed the river. Anyone with travel experience who carries luggage across the river is afraid of the journey. Fortunately, all of our team members were unwilling to be scammed by the porters. They carried their luggage themselves from the pier to the ferry and from the ferry to the train. This saved time and avoided trouble. All the passers-by praised them. At 10 AM, the train departed. The seats were very spacious, because the Tianjin-Pukou stationmaster had reserved half a car in advance, and no one else was allowed to mix in, so it was quite comfortable. After the train passed Linhuai Pass, it began to rain lightly, and the weather suddenly became cool. The train traveled between Xuzhou and Dong'an, which was the time for us to sleep.

The Train Turns into a Water-Soaked Chicken

On the 30th, several team members who got up early saw Mount Tai looming in the distance. With a shout, the entire team woke up and leaned out of the windows, all eager to see Mount Tai. But in the cloudy and rainy weather, the peaks were hidden in the clouds, which was very disappointing. After the train passed Tai'an, the rain became heavier and heavier, and the wind blew harder and harder. The roof of the train leaked, making almost the entire car wet. The team members suffered greatly, and the weather suddenly turned cold. It was necessary to wear wool or cotton clothing. Fortunately, the team members had prepared in advance and did not suffer. The train arrived at Tianjin Central Station at 10:30 AM. Zhang Jiwu (Association), Yang Junru (Dagong Bao), Kong Zhaokai (Guowen), Zhao Quan (Yong Bao), Ding Jichang (Yishi Bao), and more than ten representatives of other organizations were waiting at the station. They then took cars to Nankai Middle School and stayed in the student dormitory. Unfortunately, there were many bedbugs, and most of the team members did not sleep well. They will move to the classroom to live in, which will be more comfortable. The reception here is very thorough and meticulous, and the team members are quite satisfied.

Tilden Discusses This Year's US Professional Tennis Championships

| Talented Players Gathered, Who Knows Who Will Win? |

New York, June 14 - World-renowned tennis star Tilden, in his capacity as a professional tennis player, has made a statement regarding the National Professional Tennis Championships to be held on July 6 at Forest Hills.

Talented Players Gathered

In this competition, the former champion Kreigkau Shanlu, the runner-up Fenson Li Queke, Falake Xiangtuo, Howard Kimshan, Amman Tuo Guhe, Bao Peishan La, Hawie Shi Nagelas, Kaliute, myself, and major European players will be called upon to attend. At that time, a contest on the green lawn will be quite spectacular.

Two Good Men

I have played against both the former champion Kau Shanlu and the runner-up Li Queke. From my observations, the two have their own characteristics. Li's magical volley and Kao's comprehensive defense cannot be denied by anyone. When the two compete, Kao has a stable advantage on hard courts, and Li can win on grass or indoors. The two have met thirty times, and Kao has won twenty-four times. How their skills are, can be imagined.

The Future of the Championship

Based on a scientific perspective, the four players in this championship's semi-finals will be either Cox, Li, Hentoff, or myself. However, if major European players like Abbott, Pank, Roman, Jack, Martin, and Pollock participate, there might be some adjustments. Regardless, Cox will strive to maintain his reputation as champion. Li has long aimed to win the title, and Hentoff is talented and unwilling to be defeated. It remains unknown who will claim the championship in the future. (Reporter's note: Tilden's ambition and yearning for the throne are evident in his writing, though not explicitly stated.)

Promotion of Sports by Professionals

The employees of the customs declaration industry in the Beiyang district of this city, in order to promote sports and foster camaraderie among colleagues, have specially organized a Hornet Fitness Team, with fitness as its goal. On the 9th at 9:00 AM, a formal inaugural meeting was held at the Hat Industry Association on Huajin Road, where the team was officially established. World Snippets

— Hai Ke

Glass School Buildings

Germany has always held the highest position in the world regarding educational methods. Recently, a new school has been established with unprecedented architecture, unlike any other in the world. The walls of all classrooms are not made of brick and stone but entirely of glass. Even the bookshelves and cabinets displaying student achievements are made entirely of glass. Furthermore, the outer walls are also entirely of glass, ensuring ample sunlight in the classrooms without any lack of light. In the chemistry lab, each desk is equipped with water, electricity, and gas facilities for student convenience. There is also a large greenhouse, where flowers bloom year-round, continuously through all seasons. One classroom is equipped with a new astronomy machine, allowing students to study the stars at any time of day. Most pleasing to the students is the school's attached tavern, where they can drink alcohol. Moreover, each classroom has a washbasin. With such a modern and delightful school, students will certainly not skip classes.

Criminal Opinions

The prison authorities in New York City, USA, are seeking to improve prisons and have specially offered rewards for prisoners to submit opinion letters, criticizing the current state of prisons and suggesting improvements. The prisoners were overjoyed upon receiving this news and engaged in writing. However, people in society are discussing whether, if prison treatment is improved too much, criminals might become too comfortable, and more people might commit crimes in the future.

Questions and Answers Regarding International Affairs

— Xu Wusheng

The reason why white women are so fond of yellow men: A European woman with great vision fell in love with a handsome Chinese man. At the peak of their love, she said to the man, "My dear, I am a woman who has traveled the world. I have seen many races, but today I met you. You are the dearest person to me in my life. I cannot leave you." However, the man's thoughts about such rhetoric had already become a cliché, likely due to temporary encounters with the opposite sex. Based on the man's experience and what was imprinted in his mind, he couldn't escape the idea that Easterners are Easterners, and Westerners are Westerners. If these two sides could become one, the Yellow River would run clear. Therefore, the man forced himself to ask the woman, "What is the purpose of your love for me? And I must first state that I am a Chinese man among Eastern yellow people. Please do not forget this question."

The white woman replied, "What I love about you is your yellowness. Don't you know the color of lemons? Isn't it yellow? It is loved by people all over the world. Its color is elegant and beautiful, its nature is firm and durable, and it has lasting value, making it the most noble of fruits. You must also not forget that your China is the birthplace of Eastern culture. This culture contains endless profound philosophy. Therefore, we come to China to obtain the true truth of culture, which requires getting close to your countrymen."

Forgiving Debt and Repaying Money: A friend of an English pastor borrowed some money from him. On Sunday, he prepared to repay the money. Unexpectedly, the pastor was preaching in church, reciting the prayer, "Matthew 6:12," singing, "Forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors." The men and women in the congregation all said the same. The friend who was repaying the debt heard this prayer and thought, "This English pastor is a truly good person. He is willing to forgive my debt." Then he thought of his sick child at home and decided to use the money for medical expenses. If he repaid the pastor, he would have no money for treatment. After the service, the pastor saw his friend and said happily, "Did you bring all the money, including the interest?" The friend who was repaying the debt said to him, "What did you say in the Bible just now? You clearly said you wanted to forgive my debt. Does that mean you have given up the money I owe you? No wonder American President Hoover has the same intention towards Germany. Is it implementing the teachings of the Bible? So, the reason I don't need to repay you the money now is that I need to get medical treatment for my child first." The pastor replied, "Forgiving other people's debts is possible, but you must first repay the money you owe me. Your child's illness and the need to buy medicine and see a doctor are separate issues and have nothing to do with me." (Chou)

Records of Ye Han Cheng

— Lu Jingqing

Mr. Ye Hancheng of Nanhui is a progressive figure who studied in the East and an outstanding member of the Tongmenghui. Over the years, he has worked tirelessly for the revolution and can be said to have contributed to the party and the nation. After the European War, he studied in Berlin, expanding his knowledge. He then obtained a doctorate and served as an assistant professor at the University of Berlin. In 1920, he returned to China and took a teaching position at Peking University. When the Premier was in Guangdong, he organized the Grand Marshal's Office. Since 1926, he has been in charge of the Wuzhou Gubenzao Pharmaceutical Factory, making great achievements and praised by his friends. Recently, a celebration was held for the double auspicious birthday of Mr. and Mrs. Ye. Contemporary talents, such as Yu Youren, Niu Yongjian, Ye Chucang, Shao Lizi, Ma Junwu, Jiang Menglin, Lian Nanhu, and Chen Taoyi, all old friends, launched a celebration for Mr. Ye's birthday. Mr. Huang Renzhi composed a poem: "Unexpectedly, the events of twenty-eight years ago, nine deaths, a few young men, a hundred plans to realize a great dream, I will send the worries to the zenith of glory. This person has this disease. It is doubtful that it can be handled. The spirit is through all the senses. This intention of life to others and self-life, the day is in the middle of the hundred years." According to Mr. Renzhi and Mr. Ye, during the Guangxu period, they were all enthusiastic about the party and the country, striving to instill culture in the mainland, awaken the national soul, and open up the trend. Unfortunately, they were jealous of the Qing officials and almost sacrificed for the revolution. Now, revisiting the old Nansha, there is no feeling of looking back on the past.

The Analysis of Love

— Yunying

Great scientists can use counter-scientific methods to analyze and solve the infinite problems of the universe, but no one has ever been able to give an absolute explanation of "love." Love is originally a mysterious flower. It is produced in the garden of nature, irrigated by nature, grows naturally, bears natural fruits, but does not disappear naturally.

Love cannot take "seduction" as its starting point. Its starting point should be "sympathy."

Love cannot take "flattery" as its fertilizer. Its fertilizer should be "sincere comfort."

Love cannot take money or physical and other material conditions as its purpose. Its purpose should be "pure mutual support."

Love cannot be plundered by power. It should be demanded by justice.

Love has no trace of coercion. It is entirely a natural inspiration.

If there is a man who uses intimidation or deception to force a woman to sacrifice, this is definitely not love. What is it then?

If, between a pair of opposite sexes, what is relied upon to maintain them is not love, what will be the result?

If a man does not understand what love is, but a woman cannot but sacrifice his love, what is the reason?

No matter what encyclopedia we read, we cannot get an explanation of the above questions. However, as long as we have the opportunity to see the new film "The Killer Miss" by the Star Film Company, it will definitely give you a very accurate answer.

This article of mine is definitely not to promote "The Killer Miss" because I think the answers to these questions, apart from "The Killer Miss," can give me an explanation. I can't find it elsewhere, so I dare to say that.

Gleanings from Mr. Yu Qiaqing's Commemorative Meeting

— Ji Ping

The Shanghai giant merchant Mr. Yu Qiaqing’s 50th anniversary of his stay in Shanghai was held at the Grand China Hotel the day before yesterday. The decoration was rich and the ceremony was solemn. Mr. Yu deserves the credit for his lifelong career that contributed to the society and the country. I humbly attended this grand event and saw and heard many interesting things. I will extract one or two to share with the readers.

A conference of fellow villagers: The guests who signed in at the memorial meeting each day numbered more than 6,000. Although there were quite a few foreign guests and people from various provinces, 80-90% were Ningbo people. Most of the speakers spoke in the Ningbo dialect, and the guests also conversed in this way. Some said that this event was no different from a conference of fellow villagers. Foreign Minister Wang said that Mr. Yu was not only a Ningbo person from Ningbo, a Ningbo person from Zhejiang, but also a Ningbo person from China. The meaning behind it is worth pondering.

The interest of the speech: The speeches at the celebration were the most brilliant on the first day, and each was based on their respective positions. For example, Mayor Zhang said that Mr. Yu has made 50 years of efforts in Shanghai's business community, financial sector, and the construction of Greater Shanghai has been of great help. Foreign Minister Wang said that Mr. Yu's success lies in his efforts, for his career, for society, and for the country. He makes every effort at all times and continues to work hard for 50 years to achieve today's success. Yuan Ludeng spoke about the shipping industry. Lin Kanghou called himself a younger brother and said that Mr. Yu is 65 years old and I am 56 years old. If we each set aside 50 years, then I am only 6 years old. Isn't it a younger brother? The general idea is related to the banking industry. Ye Huijun said that Mr. Yu came to Shanghai barefoot at the age of fifteen. After 50 years of hard work, although his career was successful, he was still a poor man and a barefoot friend. Mr. Yu never puts on airs. Sometimes when he returns to Ningbo, he sits in third class and hangs out with the sailors, and he has never heard foreigners laugh at him as "Dammfull." The audience all burst into laughter.

The problem of eating: There are so many guests, so it is difficult to solve the problem of eating. This excellent event was contracted by the Deng Tuomo Hotel. A total of 12,000 Western dishes were served in two days. The hotel originally had only 40 waiters. This time, due to the insufficient distribution of work, he recruited from various restaurants. Add more than a hundred people. They all wear new D M C numbers. However, because it was newly compiled temporarily, it was difficult to command. Guests dine, originally standing. (Buffet Lunch) More than a dozen rows of long tables were placed in the Italian Hall of the Grand China Hotel. Men, women, old and young occupy the table. Stand and eat. Laughter is mixed. Not a few times. In foreign banquets or garden parties with more than a thousand people, there are often so-called standing meals. It is still an innovation in our country. Some guests have to wait for a long time to eat. There are many disputes. The business group members who maintained order announced martial law. The waiters carried the dishes. Sending staff to escort is also an interesting thing.

Poor Dancing: At 9:00 PM, the dance music was loud. The audience surrounded the surroundings. They all wanted to take a peek at the social dance. The China Tianyi Company put a strong electric light in the field to film. The average dancers were reluctant to see it. Even Miss Xiuyun, the granddaughter of the dance group director Lao Qia, was not seen in the audience. Only Lao Qia's son-in-law Jiang Yiping embraced one or two eight beauties and danced the foxtrot. He was very interested. His wife, Ms. Danru, was unhappy about it.

General Statistics: This conference can be said to be unprecedented at sea. Each department has a total of more than 350 employees. More than 8,000 visiting coupons were issued. 12,000 commemorative badges. The collected gifts exceeded 100,000 yuan, all of which were used to open the Sanbei Hospital. More than 2,000 gifts, mostly silver shields, silver cups, streamers, and couplets. As for beer, more than 400 dozen were drunk. Yili and Shegsheng, two kinds of soda, totaled more than 3,000 dozen. It's hot. This drink is especially needed for guests to cool off. Yesterday's motorcade, the Engineering Bureau initially allowed 50 vehicles as the limit. There were more to join along the way, more than 200 vehicles. Mighty and mighty, like a living tiger and dragon. Wherever it passes, traffic is cut off. Citizens sighed as a spectacle.

？？？（20）

— Xu Zhuodai

After the wife finished speaking, she left lightly. Not long after, the noise in the front room became louder again.

"Is Mr. Pan feeling unwell and lying in bed?"

"Yes, he is resting in the back room."

"I want to see him!"

Zi Liang's heart was pounding, as if a patient had met a life-threatening ghost. He didn't even have time to hide.

"Mr. Pan! Are you feeling unwell? We haven't seen each other for a long time."

"Yes!"

"What's wrong with you?"

Zi Liang thought, "I just don't like you two noisy people. Other than that, I don't feel unwell at all." So, he looked at his wife, almost saying, "Why did you say I was sick?"

"Do you have a headache?"

Zi Liang nodded. Actually, his head didn't hurt at all, but he thought that seeing you two female generals really gave him a headache, so he nodded to indicate yes.

"Does your stomach hurt?"

Zi Liang had to shake his head. He thought, "Don't ask me like a doctor, how's my appetite? How's my bowel movement?" If you ask me one by one like that, my perfectly healthy body will really get sick."

"Just a headache? That's easy!"

After saying this, she turned to his wife again:

"Call the maid to bring a glass of water!"

The wife really called the maid to pour a glass of water. Zi Liang didn't understand what she meant. Could it be that she knew massage? He saw her take out a small glass bottle from her side, removed the stopper, and poured two white pills from the bottle onto the desk:

"This is a miracle medicine specially for headaches. I often take it. It's almost always effective. Take these two pills with water, and your headache will be gone in less than ten minutes."

Commercial News

Sharp Rebound in the Gold Market Last Week in Financials

Silver Price Reduction and Stock Drop are the Main Reasons

Last week, the gold market rose sharply and rapidly, breaking through the 740 tael mark. However, the waves were turbulent, with fluctuations of more than ten taels per day, creating a confusing situation and making it difficult for people to take action. Starting from the early morning of the beginning of the week at 698.5 taels, it immediately exceeded 700 taels. Subsequently, the ups and downs were erratic. By Thursday, it had reached 742 taels, then hovered around 30 taels. This week saw a total fluctuation of 43.5 taels, with a total increase of 26.4 taels. This was due to conflicting news regarding the suspension of European war debts, resulting in unpredictable changes. Overseas silver markets continued to decline sharply, and New York stocks also trended lower. The Shanghai market's foreign exchange was quite tight (a reduction of three and a half grades). Actual transactions in banks were still lively. Chinese gold businesses were again trying to cover their short positions, but they were still in a short position. The exchange rate between the Japanese yen and gold was pressed down by 30 to 40 taels. Existing spot goods from July had not yet been completely cleared. The current cash reserves of various firms are about 30,000 bars, but the sales of bare bars are sluggish, leading to lower prices than before. The forward gold tenders increased by more than 11 taels. If the German loan is successful, the future of gold prices may fall. The general situation of the week is recorded below:

Rose 26.4 Taels Day by Day

Since Monday (6th), the standard silver price was reduced by 0.0625, and there was no market for silver prices. Almost the sterling was also reduced by one grade, and the internal situation tightened. As for the August gold tender, the initial opening fell by 5 taels, amounting to 698.5 taels, because it was heard that the US-French debt issue seemed to be settled. And the sellers were active. Soon the buyers launched an attack, and the exchange rate also loosened, immediately breaking through 710 taels. Subsequently, it was uncertain up and down and had receded within 10 taels. In the afternoon, the upward trend suddenly turned strong, and buyers were brave, and the closing price was 14.2 taels, which was 10.7 taels higher than last Saturday. However, transactions were not strong, which was actually due to the new wooden fence in the arena and the employment of outsiders as inspectors, and those without a certificate were not allowed to enter the transaction, so it aroused the opposition of various brokers, and even went to the director to question and demand the removal of foreign inspectors, the market order was chaotic for a while, and the transactions on the table were not affected, and the difference in the market throughout the day was 15.7 taels. The next day, the standard silver price was again 0.125 lower, the silver price fell by 0.375, and the sterling was again reduced by one grade. The internal market was stable, and the industry was scrambling to buy and sell. The initial opening of the gold market was 717.5 taels, a slight increase of 3.3 taels, and soon it jumped to 10 taels, amounting to 27 taels. Subsequently, the Guangdong group and hedging, etc. sold, and the price immediately fell to 18 taels. At noon, it became more moderate and remained outside 20 taels. In the afternoon, the sellers were sensitive and the exchange rate also loosened, falling by more than 10 taels to only 709 taels. The closing price was pulled to 710.09 taels, but it was slightly lower by 3.3 taels compared with the previous day. The difference in the front and rear markets was 18 taels. On Wednesday, the standard silver price rose by 0.0625, the silver market did not change, and the sterling was reduced by half a grade. The internal market was also strong, so the gold price opened with an increase of 7.1 taels, amounting to 18 taels. Also, due to the sharp drop in New York stocks, it receded from 23.5 taels to 16.5 taels, and then was taken over by a speculator named Wu, jumping more than 10 taels, to 29 taels. At noon, hedging, etc. were sold, suppressing the price by a little more than 10 taels. The closing price rebounded by 4 to 5 taels. In the afternoon, it was still firm, reaching 28.5 taels. The result was 27.1 taels, which was 16.2 taels higher than the previous day. The difference in the market throughout the day was 12.5 taels. The next day, the standard silver price fell again by 0.25, and the silver price plummeted by 0.75, so the sterling was also reduced by one grade. The internal market was very tight. Almost the gold market opened high, at 736.5 taels, and the New York stock market also fell, followed by 37.5 taels, but the Dalian group and Guangdong group, etc. sold, conceding more than 5 taels, to 32 taels. Afterwards, it frequently rose to the clouds, but the exchange rate was particularly strong, and at noon it suddenly reached 742 taels. In the afternoon, because the news of the strict handling of the Korean people's riots in Wanbaoshan came, people's hearts were frustrated, reaching 32 taels, and the closing price was 37.2 taels, which was still 10.01 taels higher than the previous day. There was only a slight fluctuation of 1 tael throughout the day. On Friday, the standard silver price was again reduced by 0.25, and the silver price also fell by 0.25, so the sterling did not change, and the internal market seemed loose. The gold market immediately fell by 8.2 taels, to 29 taels, followed by 27 taels, but the buyers were not lonely, rising to 34.4 taels, and then speculators such as Lu sold, so it receded to 27 taels. At noon, it hovered around 30 taels. In the afternoon, the selling atmosphere was very strong, suddenly falling to 24.8 taels, until the closing price was 26.7 taels, a drop of 10.05 taels compared with the previous day. In short, the air is bad and people's hearts are floating. On Saturday, the standard silver price rose by 0.1875, and the silver price rose by 0.125, so the sterling did not change, but the gold market opened high, at 33.5 taels, followed by 5.5 taels. Afterwards, it hovered on a small scale, receding to 30 taels, and at noon it was 28 taels. Until the closing price of 29.9 taels, a slight increase of 3.2 taels compared with the previous day. However, after the closing price, it continued to be done to 32 taels. In half a day, only 7.5 taels fluctuated, and the overall market did not have major changes. British and American Silver Prices Each Reduced by 125

Yesterday was Sunday. There were no reports on financial foreign exchange markets. However, the London telegraph said that a few Indians were selling, transactions were scarce, and the market was flat. After the close, the market was calm. According to the standard silver, it has rebounded, and the near and far periods have been reduced by 125, both being 13 pence 1875. The New York telegraph also received a reduction of 125, with spot goods being 2 jiao 8 fen 375, and private telegraphs also reduced by 125, being 2 jiao 8 fen 625. The market is trending strongly. The British-to-US has dropped by 03125, at 4 yuan 8 jiao 6 fen 32 parts of 21. The Japanese-to-US has dropped by 1 fen, at 49 yuan 3 jiao 8 fen. The British-to-Japanese remains at 2 shillings 0375. The Bombay spot has decreased by 2 anas, totaling 43 Robis 12 anas. The forward has also decreased by 2 anas, at 40 Robis 07 anas. The market is strong.

The Copper Cash Market is Falling Step by Step

A turnaround is expected today.

Yesterday was a bank holiday. The market was weak, and the price of cash continued to decline. The early and midday markets were both at 7 qian 2 fen 4 li and a half, a drop of 3 hao 7 xus and a half compared to the previous day. The silver demolition rebounded by 2 fen, totaling 6 fen. The early and midday markets were also the same. The value of the drafts made was 562,000 in the early market and 225,000 in the midday market. There were no transactions for banknotes in either market. The off-market banknotes were only 40,000 in the early market. Securities: Last Week's Bond Prices Decline

The trend moderates with over 9.2 million in transactions

During the past week, the spot and futures market conditions for various bond maturities in the Shanghai securities market were very active in the first half of the week. Buying and selling interest was lively, and activity in major bonds was vibrant. However, the market suddenly turned quiet in the second half of the week, with all parties adopting a wait-and-see attitude. Daily trading volume was only around 10,000 yuan, likely because the overall bond market environment was dull and bond prices were increasingly stagnant. Total turnover for the week was 9,215,500 yuan, with twenty-year customs duties being the most actively traded, accounting for 3,393,500 yuan, divided into 2,666,500 yuan for the July期 and 727,000 yuan for the August期. Twenty-year tobacco bonds amounted to 1,705,500 yuan, divided into 1,314,000 yuan for the July期 and 391,500 yuan for the August期. Other bonds were quiet, mainly because the supply of spot goods in the market was gradually decreasing and prices had risen significantly. For example, the 1920 issue amounted to 1,131,500 yuan, the 1920 customs issue to 1,094,000 yuan, Disbandment bonds to 751,500 yuan, Reorganization bonds to 614,000 yuan, the 1996 public bonds to 321,000 yuan, customs duties to 116,500 yuan, Readjustment 6% bonds to 82,000 yuan, 7-year bonds to 5,500 yuan, and Financial bonds to 5,000 yuan. Spot transactions were very few, with a total weekly turnover of 92,400 yuan, including 34,000 yuan for the 1920 customs issue, 21,400 yuan for the 1920 issue, and several thousand yuan each for Disbandment 7-year bonds. In addition, 20 shares of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange were traded unexpectedly. Due to the thriving business of the exchange, its price had risen by 16 yuan and 9 jiao compared to the end of last year. Regarding the price trends of various bonds during the past week, although the overall bond market environment was quiet, bond prices had risen significantly in the recent month or so, so the buying interest in the market was not as strong as before. At the same time, the availability of actual goods made it difficult to sell short. As a result, the supply and demand situation was balanced, and the daily trend was slightly weak, with a stronger decline on Tuesday. The second half of the week was in a state of consolidation, with little change throughout. As a result, compared to the previous week, except for continued increases in spot prices for the 1920 customs, the 1920 issue, and the 1920 opening issue, most other bond futures declined, with the 1920 tobacco issue falling by more than 1 yuan, and the rest only by about five or six jiao. Judging from the bond market situation, it will likely remain stable for the time being and is not expected to experience significant fluctuations. Cotton Yarn: Last Week's Yarn Market Dull and Lifeless

Fine Yarn Exports Still Strong

Sales of 10-Count Coarse Yarn Very Sluggish

Last week, the cotton yarn market was extremely dull. Large short sellers were reportedly dumping goods daily, causing increasing panic. As for actual sales, seeing the sharp decline in futures prices, even if there was interest, buyers dared not proceed. However, trade in Japanese export yarn continued briskly, with large quantities of Zhonghua brand yarn already shipped out. A significant portion of speculators were also active. However, sales of 10-count coarse yarn were very sluggish. There were approximately 23,000 to 24,000 bales of inventory in the yarn and cloth warehouses. With such a large quantity of goods pressing on the market, it was difficult to boost prices in the short term. Nevertheless, with the overseas yarn market still rising, market sentiment could tighten somewhat. The spot market for 16-count and 20-count yarn was extremely tight, resulting in very firm selling prices. The future situation is difficult to predict. The standard yarn market was flat during the week, with slight increases of two or three qian in each month. There was a slight increase mid-week, but it fell again at the weekend due to the decline in American cotton. Total turnover for the week was 150,350 bales. Various merchants purchased 5,686 bales of spot yarn, while fellow traders took in 2,400 bales. The market for Japanese yarn was very firm. Shenxin Factory opened forward sales of approximately 5,000 to 6,000 bales of Zhonghua brand yarn for shipment to Japan. Cotton Market Listless Last Week

Hankou Standard Near-Month Down Seven or Eight Qian

American Cotton Down 100 Points Per Pound

The cotton market has been even calmer since last week, with nothing exciting to report. Although sources of supply were scarce, the current cotton needs of various factories were also quiet, and yarn prices were weak, leading to disappointing sales. As for foreign cotton, the situation was exceptionally pessimistic, causing increasingly weak sentiment. Fortunately, gold prices remained firm, making it difficult to import large quantities of foreign cotton, so the market has not yet shown any weaknesses. However, most people have a bearish outlook on far-month new cotton. Only the Japanese merchant Dongmian Trading Company purchased a large quantity, approximately over 100,000 dan. The intention is to sell foreign cotton and purchase Chinese cotton, which is more cost-effective. However, recently, reports have been received from various local areas that excessive rainfall is causing concern, and if it clears up quickly, the impact will be minor. But if it continues unabated, it may be detrimental to the cotton seedlings. Hankou standard near-month prices fell by seven or eight qian due to a lack of buyers, while far-month prices remained flat. Turnover totaled 267,700 dan. Supplies included 4,570 dan of flower clothing and 90 bales of general-grade cotton. Few factories purchased new cotton. American cotton fell 100 points per pound compared to the previous week. Grain and Rice Markets Tightening Consistently Downriver

New Zhabei

Yesterday, due to light rain, the appetite for rice suddenly increased, with more retail shortages and limited fluctuations in large wholesale markets. The price of top-quality thick japonica rice remained at the previous level. Second-grade rice from previous crops rose nearly one foot. Early and late rice remained relatively stable, with high-quality rice slightly lower by half a foot. The outgoing traffic of foreign superior grade rice was slightly scarce, with no gains or losses. Superior grade rice from domestic ports was cleared upon arrival, and the situation slightly improved by several points. Tongbian distilleries still had strong demand, and prices rose by about one foot. Boats arriving from the west included Changshu, Liyang, Jiangyin, Kunshan, Wangting, Jiaoli, Sijing, and Liantang, totaling seventeen or eight boats.

South Market

Although supplies from various merchants were thin, retail sales in urban and rural stores were sluggish. This was due to continuous light rain, which weakened sentiment, and prices also eased accordingly. The thick japonica market remained temporarily unchanged. The arrival of thin rice was limited, and appetite remained thin. Street sales seemed expensive and showed signs of weakening, resulting in a shortage of about one foot. The outgoing traffic of foreign superior grade rice was very limited, with a soft appearance. Yin-transformed rice had strong buying interest, and the overall market rose by one or two feet. The production price of foreign rice was unprofitable, and sentiment was upward. Sales were driven by local buyers, and market prices were tightening.

Sugar Market: After Plate-Drawing, Sugar Prices Tend to Firm Again

Yesterday, due to the holiday, there were no reports from the producing areas. Although plate-drawing transactions in the guild market were not high, the market sentiment was exceptionally strong. The transaction price for No. 24 Dutch raw white sugar was 10 taels 0.075 to 0.08 taels. The supply of coarse-grained sugar was even scarcer, and prices were higher, reaching 11 taels. The back market called for 10 taels 0.05 taels, and medium-grade white sugar was 10 taels 0.04 taels. The market situation was strong. Trading in Japanese sugar was active, and the market also rose slightly. N mark was 10 taels 0.075 taels, YT mark was 10 taels 0.07 taels, new goods were 10 taels 0.0725 taels to 0.075 taels, SH mark was 10 taels 0.065 taels, YRO mark was 10 taels 0.055 taels to 0.05875 taels, YP mark was 11 taels 0.075 taels. The market was firm. Nan Shenglong opened a plate for 200 bags of merchant-bowl green sugar, priced at 8.4 yuan, which was reportedly purchased exclusively by a certain merchant.

World Route

Pao Ke 22nd

Market News

The Da Xin Silk and Satin Shop at the corner of San Ma Road and Shi Road, starting from the 5th of this month, will be selling a large batch of new and expensive summer clothing materials at reduced prices to reward customers. Therefore, although there have been heavy rains in recent days, the business of the shop has not decreased slightly. The bargain department set up by the shop offers various new and unique silk materials at even cheaper prices, only selling them at cloth prices. Their spirit of sacrifice is truly astonishing. The shop previously commissioned tens of thousands of elegantly made silver-faced round fans, which were well received after being distributed to various circles. It is now heard that the fan supply is almost exhausted, and they are continuing to commission more to replenish the supply.

The Guanshengyuan Food Company declares that their company has more than ten years of experience in manufacturing fresh fruit syrups. Through years of improvement, the fresh fruit syrups have a trend of dominating the market in terms of both quality and reputation. Recently, at the peak of the season, the sales of the fresh fruit syrups have not only increased sharply in this city's market, but also various cities in other provinces are successively wholesaling them without interruption. In terms of manufacturing, they are currently working day and night to rush production.

The Anlu Cotton Weaving Factory at the corner of Nanjing Road and Shi Road declares that their factory will hold a 20% discount promotion starting from July 7th, selling all kinds of bath towels, bathrobes, bed sheets, curtain materials, quilt covers, shirts, undershirts, cloth, mosquito nets, etc. at 20% off.

The Shanghai Competition Company at No. 452 Fuyou Road in the city declares that their company's competition games have been praised by all sectors of society, resulting in increased sales. Recently, to cater to the psychology of society, they have created a hunting game, the interest of which is strong and the ingenuity of the design is unmatched by any other toy. Currently, in order to promote business, each set is sold for only 80 cents. Bulk wholesale purchases will be offered with even more favorable prices. The Commercial Press and major bookstores in this city are selling on their behalf.

The Dahua Woolen Factory declares that its expanded preparatory office held its fourth founders' preparatory meeting at the Atlantic Restaurant at 6 p.m. on the day before yesterday (July 9th). Wang Xiaolai, Xiang Songmao, Yu Guozhen, Gu Jiuru, Chen Zipu, Lu Xingzhuang, Wang Caiyun, Zhang Shenzhi, Xu Juetang, Ding Yongkui, Lu Wenshao, Xu Nuqi, Jia Yaoqing, (Gu Jiuru on behalf of) Wang Honghui, Sun Shouchun and others attended. Gu Jiuru chaired the meeting and Wang Honghui served as the recorder. The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting, the preparatory situation, and the negotiation process of the machinery factory base, etc. Then Xiang Maosong, Yang Jian, Zhang Shenzhi, Lu Xingzhuang and others expressed their opinions and jointly discussed issues related to machinery, and resolved to set the period from July 15 to August 15 as the stock collection date, and designated the Guohua National Goods, Shanghai Kenye Four Banks, and Yuanda, Ankang, Zikang, and Shunkang Four Money Shops as stock collection agencies.

The Miaoji Department Store on North Sichuan Road declares that since the company started its tenth anniversary grand discount and lottery promotion on July 1st for 31 days, although the weather has been unusually hot in recent days, customers have been enthusiastically buying goods, to the point where it feels like the threshold is being worn through. This is because the quality of the goods is excellent and the prices are reasonable, which is incomparable to those who merely pay lip service. Moreover, this year's lottery prizes have been greatly increased compared to last year, with 50 grand prizes and 5,000 small prizes. Buying one yuan of goods gives the hope of winning a 100 yuan first prize. The company also just received a large batch of summer daily necessities yesterday, the beauty of the texture and the novelty of the patterns are truly rare. Originally intended to be kept until after the discount, in order to reward customers, they are also being sold at reduced prices.

The Yuanlai Run Candle Shop in Dongxinqiao declares that the shop has been open for more than ten years, selecting high-quality asphalt and exquisitely crafting official ceremonial candles, which are sold in various provinces and have a good reputation. Now, a factory has been established to add production of the high-quality, effective, national product Living Buddha brand plague-preventing, pest-repelling mosquito incense. Not long after its release, those who go to buy it are constantly connected. Currently, the manager, in order to expand the sales of national goods, has hired Mr. Chen to set up agents everywhere, so as to avoid the customers' arduous journeys. Patriotic gentlemen, why not try to buy it? Constantly burning it on the desk truly has the effect of preventing immunity and avoiding plague.

The Lao Zhenghe Dyeing Factory declares that the factory has been open for decades, and the dyed goods are exquisite, with a long history. In order to give preferential treatment to patrons, the factory issues a 30% discount pre-order voucher once a year. This year's session has already begun issuing them. It is heard that the fixed number is only 2,000 vouchers, so hurry to purchase them.

Theater News

The Tianyi Film Company declares that in order to start shooting talking movies in Shanghai, they specially purchased the Movietone machine from the United States. This machine arrived yesterday, consisting of more than a dozen huge boxes, including a truck, which is the most important. It is said that it is used to install all the cameras and microphones when shooting on location, and it can also generate electricity on the car and start the motor. Also, forty or so light bulbs were delivered the day before. The company's first talking movie is "Spring Colors of the Theater", the plot of which is extraordinarily lively, and it will be starting shooting soon. The second movie is "Shanghai Miss", which has also begun preparation. It is also heard that the company will exclusively undertake the shooting of talking movies for the 50th anniversary celebration of Yu Qiaqing's stay in Shanghai. The celebration at the Dahua Hotel on the first day and the grand automobile parade on the second day will all be filmed.

Publishing News

The Wanshang Bookstore declares that it has hired Mr. Zhang Yuqing to visit and investigate for many years to compile the latest Shanghai City Map, which is printed in five colors, with precise and detailed annotations, and precise zoning. All boundaries, roads, proposed roads, streets, streetcars, trackless trolleys, direct connections, as well as government offices, consulates, police stations, schools, etc. are all clearly marked. It is heard that it has already begun distribution, and each map is sold for only 30 cents. All major bookstores sell it.

The YMCA Bookstore on Museum Road declares that in order to promote swimming, it has specially translated and printed the 22 illustrated explanations of swimming techniques recently written by Miss Helen Wainwright, a first-class American swimmer, to give to the people of the country. The important parts of swimming and the correct posture when diving are photographed as much as possible in the illustrations, and white lines are used to indicate the rising and falling of hands and feet. Not only are they detailed and clear, but the slender figure can also express the graceful beauty of a dancer when swimming, which is a good model for beginners in swimming. The book is exquisitely printed on copperplate paper, and the price is 40 cents per copy.
